  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_370c8960-b030-44e7-b27a-103c1b36cff0'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <span id="freeText12257876530247491167" style="display:none"><i>This is a previously published edition of ISBN 9780062878021. There, witches like Lou are hunted. They are feared. And they are burned.<br /><br />Sworn to the Church as a Chasseur, Reid Diggory has lived his life by one principle: <i>thou shalt not suffer a witch to live.</i> His path was never meant to cross with Lou's, but a wicked stunt forces them into an impossible union—holy matrimony.<br /><br />The war between witches and Church is an ancient one, and Lou's most dangerous enemies bring a fate worse than fire. Unable to ignore her growing feelings, yet powerless to change what she is, a choice must be made.<br /><br />And love makes fools of us all.</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1668417-two-questions-1-are-there-any-steamy">Two questions:
1) Are there any steamy scenes?
I&#39;m getting tired of books where the love story between the main characters is almost platonic. Only kisses. Sex is part of a relationship, so I don&#39;t understand why most of the books avoid the topic. It doesn&#39;t have to be explicit. My God, no!
2) How many books will there be?

p.s about question 1, it&#39;s not a critique to the book per se, because I&#39;m loving it, FYI.</a>
</div>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Sex is NOT always part of a relationship (congrats on being acephobic!), especially not when teenagers are involved (which I'm assuming is the case he<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Sex is NOT always part of a relationship (congrats on being acephobic!), especially not when teenagers are involved (which I'm assuming is the case here, as it's labeled YA)! If you want sex in books, there is a whole entire genre out there for you - they're called adult romance novels. Those of us who don't want to read about sex deserve a space, too.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

I know that La Voisin was a french fortune-te<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I think the general assumption is that she's the equivalent of La Dame des Sorcières for the Dame Rouge? I know that La Voisin was a french fortune-teller in the 17th century, and that it literally translates to "The Neighbor" so I'm getting that vibe, otherwise La Voisin was not previously mentioned in the novel. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_2792152963" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2792152963" />
    <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/65321843-a"><img alt="✨ A ✨ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604503440p2/65321843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2792152963?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨ A ✨ " href="/user/show/65321843-a">✨ A ✨ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780062971135" href="/book/show/44890115-serpent-dove">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone who loved Nina and Matthias from SoC</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=explicit-ya">explicit-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=five-stars">five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=arcs-e-arcs-alcs">arcs-e-arcs-alcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=all-the-stars-in-the-sky">all-the-stars-in-the-sky</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=re-read-in-2020">re-read-in-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=2019-release">2019-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=debut">debut</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2792152963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15332584701266035928"><u>First Read</u> <i>July 2019</i><br/><br/>Few things compare to that feeling you get after finishing a book that lived up to your expectations. Ever since I read the blurb of this book <i>I knew</i> I was going to love this and <b>I WAS NOT DISSAPOINTED</b>.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517568226ra/24988253.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It had everything I adore:<br/><br/><b>• addictive; easy writing <br/>• enemies-to-lovers <br/>• marriage of convenience <br/>• witch/witch hunter romance <br/>• slow burn<br/>• intricate magical system <br/>• heart warming female friendship <br/>• morally grey characters <br/>• inner battle of right and wrong</b><br/><br/>In the land of Belte</span>
  <span id="freeText15332584701266035928" style="display:none"><u>First Read</u> <i>July 2019</i><br><br>Few things compare to that feeling you get after finishing a book that lived up to your expectations. Ever since I read the blurb of this book <i>I knew</i> I was going to love this and <b>I WAS NOT DISSAPOINTED</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517568226ra/24988253.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It had everything I adore:<br><br><b>• addictive; easy writing <br>• enemies-to-lovers <br>• marriage of convenience <br>• witch/witch hunter romance <br>• slow burn<br>• intricate magical system <br>• heart warming female friendship <br>• morally grey characters <br>• inner battle of right and wrong</b><br><br>In the land of Belterra witches are burned at the stake and the Chasseur (Witchhunters), with the Archbishop as their leader, are ruthless. Their number one rule: <i>Thou shalt not suffer a witch to live.</i><br><br>Two years ago Lou left her coven (for reasons I shan't go into) and was forced to live a life of suppressing her magical nature and living in constant vigilence. She has to do what she can to survive. That being: lie, steal and kill if necessary. For life is hard in the city of Cesarine, especially for a woman. <br><br>She's managed to live for two years undetected. She was careful... up until one burglary (gone wrong) set the wheels in motion. <br><br>With the Chasseur on her tail and enemies of her past close on her heels, Lou slips up <i>again</i> and ends up in a compromising position with the Captain of the Chasseur. The Archbishop comes up with a solution: Lou can either go to prison for the rest of her life or she can marry the Captain and save his virtuous reputation. <br><br>Lou, being the smart girl she is, chooses marriage to the handsome Captain Diggory ; ). Being married to a Chasseur also grants her the protection she desperately needs from those who (also) hunt her.<br><br>Reid Diggory is a dedicated witch hunter. Despite his views on witches, he is honorable and loyal. It was such a pleasure reading about him. He is so set in his ways and it was amazing to see him loosen up and change.<br><br>The beginning was really funny as neither of them trusted the other and they were always bickering. Watching as Reid and Lou's relationship slowly blossomed, how they opened up and became more than two people stuck in an unwanted marriage was so beautiful. <br><br><b>
  <i>I knew who you were. I knew what you believed . . . and I fell in love with you anyway.</i>
</b><br><br>Their relationship reminded me so much of Matthias and Nina from <i>Six of Crows</i>. So if you loved those two, you're gonna love this!!!<br><br>I'd actually tag this as more of a New Adult than YA. <br>A warning for the youngins or for anyone not comfortable with it: <b>there is an explicit sex scene.</b> Kinda like ACOMAF. <br><br>The romance is a big part of this story but Lou has a part to play in the war between humans and witches and we're always made aware of what could happen if Lou's enemies were to find her. <br><br><br>This whole story revolves around the Church against the Witches. I liked that <b>neither side was portrayed as comepletly good or comepletly bad.</b> <br><br><blockquote>Each side despicable—a twisted perversion of what should’ve been. Each side suffering. Each side capable of great evil. And then there was me.</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>I looked around at the worshippers once more—the men and women who pleaded for mercy and cried for my blood on the same breath. How could both be in their hearts?</blockquote><br><br>One of the most important things for me when reading is whether I connect with the characters. And I feel like the author did a fantastic job in that regard. I felt their joy and their inner turmoil and by the end I would give an organ for any of these precious characters. <br><br><i>
  <b>They might’ve all been hypocrites, but I was the biggest of all.</b>
</i><br><br>I just loved everything about this book. The romance; the action; the plot twists — IT WAS BRILLIANTLY DONE. <br><br>I could go on and on about how much I love this book but I think I'll stop now.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526380016ra/25541958.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Publication Date: 3 September 2019</b><br><br><u>
  <i>Quotes might change after final publication</i>
</u><br><br><i>Many thanks to edelweiss for providing me with an e-arc in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><u>Second Read</u> <i>April 2020</i><br><br>I told myself I'd just read a few chapters and next thing I know, I was 300 pages in! <br><br>The writing was just as addictive as the first time. I love Lou's personality, she's an awesome MC. And as y'all already know, I'm trash for Reid. And Ansel is such a sweet cinnamon roll, this book would be nothing without him<br><br>I don't know what possessed me to read this now. There's still four months until the next book comes out (!!!!!). <br><br>I'm probably going to reread this book again and again in the future. <br><br><i>‹ Thank you to the publishers for sending me a finished copy of this book ›</i><br><br>____<br><b>My pre-review thoughts on:</b><br>Book 2 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2904545236" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood and Honey</a><br>Book 3 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3241143014" rel="nofollow noopener">Untitled</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15332584701266035928" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2708086017" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2708086017" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2708086017?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=coverly-love">coverly-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2019">2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2708086017" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13394092369699047422"><blockquote>
  <i>“Now move, or I swear to God, I will strip naked right here and dance the bourree!”<br/>I thrust my hands on my hips and looked at him expectantly.<br/>He didn’t even glance at the people around us. […]<br/>Instead, he kept his eyes trained on mine, a slow smirk spreading across his face.<br/>“Do it.”</i>
</blockquote><br/>Don't judge me! I can feel your judgement! I know, I know, I liked a YA fantasy, not even in spite of the romance but <i>because</i> of it. What is the world coming to?<br/><br/>I gotta say this right because many people I interact</span>
  <span id="freeText13394092369699047422" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>“Now move, or I swear to God, I will strip naked right here and dance the bourree!”<br />I thrust my hands on my hips and looked at him expectantly.<br />He didn’t even glance at the people around us. […]<br />Instead, he kept his eyes trained on mine, a slow smirk spreading across his face.<br />“Do it.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Don't judge me! I can feel your judgement! I know, I know, I liked a YA fantasy, not even in spite of the romance but <i>because</i> of it. What is the world coming to?<br /><br />I gotta say this right because many people I interact with on Goodreads will not like this book and under different circumstances I would probably be one of them. I really don't want any more of those "I read this because of you and it sucks" comments. So let me just say that this book was sold to me as a paranormal romance, not a fantasy, and I think it was pretty damn thrilling on that front. I got what I went in expecting.<br /><br />This kind of love/hate sexy banter romance works really well for me. I especially liked Lou, which I think helped the whole thing, to be honest. Her witty comebacks and refusal to sit down and behave made the story even more fun. <br /><br />I am fairly certain the main issue for most people will be the world of the novel. I'm not even sure what it's supposed to be. It’s some sorta like France fantasy world where people speak French, but it’s not exactly France-France. Yes, I know, I describe things so well. But I don't know what else to say. It's a made-up world and I don't think we're supposed to say it's France, but like, psst, it's also basically France. And it mixes some medieval views on women with more modern attitudes just in case you weren't confused enough.<br /><br />But, you know what? I didn't really care. I had a lot of fun reading it. The banter, the steaminess, even the whole witches vs witch hunters plot held my attention. That's the central story line. I won't give away how it happens, but Reid is a witch hunter and he is forced by the archbishop to marry Lou who is, unbeknownst to him, a witch. The two of them hate each other, but of course things are about to change. It's exciting!<br /><blockquote>
  <i>I knew what came next. I recognized the faint brush of energy against my skin, the familiar thrumming in my ears.<br />Magic.<br />Then came the screams.</i>
</blockquote><br />I do find myself wondering if the sequel can possibly be as good. This book drags out the tension through 500+ pages (which is too long) and by the end it's kinda been played out. While the witch aspect is somewhat interesting, I do not think I want to read another 500-page novel about just that. I guess I'll see.<br /><br /><a href="http://emilymay.me" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/EmilyMayTheBookGeek" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13394092369699047422" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3035252167" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="NReads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34369915-nreads"><img alt="NReads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600781665p2/34369915.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NReads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NReads" href="/user/show/34369915-nreads">NReads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3035252167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8039993711352170245">I know I know this does not have the qualities of a 5 star book. The magic system is nonsense and undeveloped. I have never read fanfiction in my life but this book sure felt like one. However I really really enjoyed it. Reid reminds me so much of myself because I too was raised into a family where there were no curses, and even as an adult now it still feels kinda awkward when someone curses near me.</span>

<div id="review_3155316174" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3155316174" />
    <a title="Kat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/100759205-kat"><img alt="Kat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603130096p2/100759205.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3155316174?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat" href="/user/show/100759205-kat">Kat</a>
      </span>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3155316174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5103454115197416129">it seems almost wrong to rate this bc it feels like i'm reviewing a fan fiction that i read at 3 am<br/><br/>there are a bunch of complaints i have about the craft of this book, but at the same time it was a whirlwind of a story that kept me wildly entertained even as i physically stopped myself from rolling my eyes every other chapter. <br/><br/>therefore, it sits right between a one (for quality) and a three (for fun).<br/><br/>although if i EVER see the phrase "big titty liddy" again it's on sight</span>

<div id="review_3067989751" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3067989751" />
    <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments"><img alt="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554228831p2/67920559.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3067989751?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments">Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">everyone, including your grandma</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=fantastical-creatures">fantastical-creatures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=forbidden-fruit">forbidden-fruit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=hype-is-real">hype-is-real</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=i-like-big-books-and-i-cannot-lie">i-like-big-books-and-i-cannot-lie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=its-getting-hot-in-here">its-getting-hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=arranged-marriage">arranged-marriage</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=never-forget">never-forget</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=thin-line-between-love-and-hate">thin-line-between-love-and-hate</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3067989751" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2064640849355062030"><i>
  <b>"It doesn’t end in death. It ends in hope."</b>
</i> <br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559506.gif' width='600' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559507.gif' width='600' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559508.gif' width='600' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559509.gif' width='600' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/> <br/><b>Let me tell you about my favourite NA fantasy book of 2019. </b> <br/>_______________<br/><br/><u>
  <b>A Story About A Witch Getting Hitched But <i>Much</i> More. </b>
</u><br/><i>Serpent and Dove</i> stole my heart in so many ways and all I want to do is go back and read it all over again. This lush tale full of magic and intrigue is wildly imaginative but soft at the same time and if you're a fan of romance + fantasy, I highly recommend trying this! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1575514627i/28559700._SY540_.jpg' width='600' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <a href='https://www.instagram.com/gabriella.bujdoso/?hl=en' rel='nofollow noopener'>©</a><br/><br/>The sales pitch; <br/>- enemies to lovers<br/>- k</span>
  <span id="freeText2064640849355062030" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"It doesn’t end in death. It ends in hope."</b>
</i> <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559506.gif" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559507.gif" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559508.gif" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559509.gif" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><b>Let me tell you about my favourite NA fantasy book of 2019. </b> <br>_______________<br><br><u>
  <b>A Story About A Witch Getting Hitched But <i>Much</i> More. </b>
</u><br><i>Serpent and Dove</i> stole my heart in so many ways and all I want to do is go back and read it all over again. This lush tale full of magic and intrigue is wildly imaginative but soft at the same time and if you're a fan of romance + fantasy, I highly recommend trying this! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1575514627i/28559700._SY540_.jpg" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a href="https://www.instagram.com/gabriella.bujdoso/?hl=en" rel="nofollow noopener">©</a><br><br>The sales pitch; <br>- enemies to lovers<br>- kickass heroines <br>- lovable side characters (ansel is the floofliest cinnamon roll) <br>- THE ONE BED TROPE™<br>- witches and witchhunters <br>- one badass song about a lady named Big Titty Liddy. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><br>“I know if you aren’t swearing or singing about well-endowed barmaids, something is wrong.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I honestly inhaled this and if it weren't for actually having to adult, I would have finished it in one sitting. Before I get into the crooks of my review, let's meet our two main characters; <br><br>Lou: <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559510.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br>Reid: <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575513274ra/28559511.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>If there's one thing about this book that completely sold me was the fact that I loved so many characters. Especially these two! The characters in this book had me crying, laughing and turning every page like an addict. Lou stayed true to herself throughout the entire book and was never sorry for being a badass female! I enjoyed her company right from the beginning and it was such a journey to watch her story unfold. Enter Reid... Reid was the horniest mess all encapsulated within the perfect gentleman. He was everything, to be honest. For all those people that mentioned their dynamic is so similar to Nina and Matthias from Six of Crows... you're absolutely right. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You really think I could knock two fully grown men unconscious?” <br>My husband’s reply came instantaneously. “Yes.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Their banter was off the charts, and their chemistry practically flew off the page. Because this book was told in dual POV's, I thought it was going to be a problem to distinguish two separate voices, but that was not the case. Both these characters had such a wonderful character development throughout the story and even better, was seeing them grow together. I do have to say that this is completely a New Adult book, and not a YA. Reid and Lou definielty get hot and heavy ;) <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When you weren’t in bed, I thought maybe—maybe you’d—” <br>“Left?” I said shrewdly. “It’s still on the agenda.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>For those who know my reviews, you know that I often fall into the overhype trap. I get very excited about books that have very high ratings and come in highly recommended, but then end up disappointed. I think I've finally found the winner, folks. The world-building (a lavish french renaissance-esque setting with a hub full of of illegal magic, a pleasure house with a mysterious lady, and the men of the church) was fantastic, and embedded within the story rather than separated by info-dumps. There were so many plot twists and character arcs that I was invested in more than just the romance between Reid and Lou, the story itself was fan-fucking-tastic. Truly such a magnificent debut!<b> It was so easy to love this book. </b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Can you put something on?” He waved a hand in my direction, the other firmly pressed against his eyes. “I can’t talk to you when you’re sitting there—sitting there—” <br>“Naked?” <br>His teeth clamped together with an audible snap. “Yes.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I didn't want this story to end to put it plainly. I loved it so much that I'm just going to ignore the randomness of the last couple of chapters (hehe). One shoutout that I would also like to mention is the fact that this book had LGBT characters but didn't make it a big deal or put any spotlight on them. It was briefly mentioned as a passing comment that Coco had female lovers and then when the fucking Prince of the kingdom all but asked if Reid and Lou wanted to join Coco and him on a sexcapade??! Hell yes to queer characters that don't have "being queer" as their major character trait. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1575514700i/28559715._SX540_.jpg" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a href="https://missescara.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">©</a><br><br>This is going on my all time favourites shelf and I need the second book yesterday.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2064640849355062030" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2864066182" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2864066182" />
    <a title=" Teodora " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69603149-teodora"><img alt=" Teodora " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582144281p2/69603149.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2864066182?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Teodora " class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Teodora " href="/user/show/69603149-teodora"> Teodora </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/50360622-serpent-dove">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=on-app">on-app</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=2019-releases">2019-releases</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=adult-new-adult">adult-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69603149-teodora?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2864066182" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer541639585462558654">5/5 ⭐<br/><br/><b>Full review on my Blog:</b> <a href='https://thedacianshewolf.home.blog/2020/05/25/serpent-dove-serpent-dove-1-by-shelby-mahurin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dacian She-Wolf</a> 🐺<br/><br/><i>
  <b>This book's mood song match - <a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Vo7lareN1CM' rel='nofollow noopener'>Witching Hour by In This Moment</a></b>
</i><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1587376525i/29324229._SY540_.jpg' width='292' height='422' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When other girls were playing with their dolls, pretending to be princesses like Rapunzel or Cinderella or whatever, I was hiding in my secret place aka a huge linden tree at the very back of my family’s orchard and pretending that I had the ability to control the elements.<br/><br/>I was basically running around pretending I’m flying on a stick, bending the wind at my will and “magically” t</span>
  <span id="freeText541639585462558654" style="display:none">5/5 ⭐<br><br><b>Full review on my Blog:</b> <a href="https://thedacianshewolf.home.blog/2020/05/25/serpent-dove-serpent-dove-1-by-shelby-mahurin/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dacian She-Wolf</a> 🐺<br><br><i>
  <b>This book's mood song match - <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Vo7lareN1CM" rel="nofollow noopener">Witching Hour by In This Moment</a></b>
</i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1587376525i/29324229._SY540_.jpg" width="292" height="422" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When other girls were playing with their dolls, pretending to be princesses like Rapunzel or Cinderella or whatever, I was hiding in my secret place aka a huge linden tree at the very back of my family’s orchard and pretending that I had the ability to control the elements.<br><br>I was basically running around pretending I’m flying on a stick, bending the wind at my will and “magically” talking to my dog (she was basically playing witch with me every day and I swear sometimes I could hear her speaking because I was able to “cast a spell” on her).<br><br>Even though it is not exactly how people in general picture witches and magic and spells and stuff Serpent &amp; Dove was the perfect book for the witchling me because magic comes in all forms, sizes and colours. And for the grown-ass witch I am today (because I still love to think I can do magic) it is still something that warms my heart. <br><br>For real, every time I read or see something regarding witches or magic my brain cells feel the need to go wild like:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1586502683ra/29264948.gif" width="273" height="328" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Important things I learned from this book:</b><br><br>- Don’t judge someone because you don’t understand them – not all the good is always entirely good and not all the bad is entirely bad;<br>- Boys are allowed to be shy and prude, girls are allowed to be daring and bold (and a bit nasty);<br>- Love is a powerful kind of magic and it is not bound by blood or forged by papers – it’s a wild being who gets to be tamed only when one believes it's true.<br><br>I truly loved this book, maybe until the verge of a tiny obsession. I mean, I was sure I was going to <i>like</i> it because I fell in love with that cover (and if you know me, then you know that covers play a big role in my choice of a book). I wasn’t expecting to love this book <i>that</i> much.<br><br>The action was lively and very well structured, based on the gruesome history of the witch hunt in the Middle Age, when all women were prone to be witches and burned on a stick immediately. In the name of God, of course. <i>Duh.</i><br><br>I will never ever in a million and two and a half years understand <i>why</i> do people oppress other people only because they are different. People are allowed to believe in anything they want to believe. We must be the masters of our own lives, we cannot let others tell us how to live and in what to believe. <br>Own it, people or someone else would own it for you.<br><br>Okay so, the witches are, in most of the cases, women.<br><br>In this book, there are two types of witches: <b>Dames Blanche</b>, whose magic demand balance of nature, and <b>Dames Rouge</b>, whose magic is in their blood (they perform blood magic that doesn’t demand a sacrifice to keep the balance with nature).<br><br><b>Lou</b> is a Dame Blanche. <b>Coco</b> is a Dame Rouge.<br><br>Although they were supposed to hate each other, they became <s>friends</s> sisters. And they would go to hell and back for each other because this is a book about powerful women and about sisterhood and love.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>“If she was destined to burn in Hell, I would burn with her.”</b>
</i><br><br><br>Lou ran away from her coven because she was afraid to fulfil the one thing she was conceived for: to die. So she turns into a thief and a mischief.<br><br>Everything goes upside down when she meets Reid, the very boss of the anti-witch squad. He’s truly annoying in his religious indoctrination. Truly annoying, almost blind at everything concerning that matter. But he’s also very tall and handsome so I could totally see where this was going to go, honestly. And he’s a good man, kind and caring. He's real. Like, damn, he’s got them all, okay? He’s basically like the sweetest raspberry jam in the pantry.<br><br>I just love Lou and Reid together. He’s so serious and lives guided by his honour and she’s so vulgar and daring and she drives him mad. But when they fall for each other, they see through each other’s acts. And they fall deeper.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>“And here I was – pouring my foolish heart out to you.”</b>
</i><br><br><br>Also, speaking of which, let me tell you how much I loved the fact that Lou and Coco are so <b>vulgar</b> and so <b>daring</b> and <b>foul-mouthed</b> and so unafraid to actually be sexual beings.<br><br><i>It Is InNaPrOpIaTe FoR a WoMaN tO bE tHaT iMoRaL.</i><br><br>Well, shit. Says who?<br>Just take a look at those two she-devils singing pub drinking songs about big-chested women (<i>Big Titty Liddy</i> – a bop, I want it in Billboard 100 ASAP).<br><br>Look at them saying everything they want to say, without censoring themselves. Look at them going for it without a single shit given. Judge them if you dare, but you won’t be able to stop them. Because they know how to carry themselves with pride. Because they know no shame. Fucking superb, don't you think?<br><br><br><i>
  <b>“She revelled in their disapproval.”</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1586502683ra/29264949.gif" width="413" height="232" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is love and hate and betrayal and plot-twists and everything you need in life just between the pages of this book. I really, really loved it. The characters are amazing, all of them. I loved Lou with that foul-mouth of hers, I loved Coco with her wickedly brave heart, I loved Reid with his pure heart and that stick up his arse and I truly loved babyboy Ansel who was the sweetest sweetheart of them all.<br><br>Of course, there is a religious touch to the story and a pagan one, men being the embodiment of God’s will and women being Satan or whatever. There is also empowerment going on there, feminist shit and all. There’s, actually, a lot going on there. And I loved it all.<br><br>Honestly, go and read this book. It’s been so good I almost devoured it. Yeah, there might be a slight chance not to like it, but there is an even higher one you’ll actually enjoy it very much. So go! Go for it and don’t forget to tell me how you felt about it afterwards! There’s love and hate waiting for you in there, so you’ll experience an experience, so to say.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>“Now, there was only a woman. And she was small. And she was frightened. And she was strong.”</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1586502813i/29264955.png" width="300" height="413" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>(<a href="https://urcdn.eu/styles/f49419d8-6f8e-4186-9401-5ba376a7f83d_original?b" rel="nofollow noopener">Book-styled</a>)</span>
  <a data-text-id="541639585462558654" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2938648360" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Nilufer Ozmekik" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53701594-nilufer-ozmekik"><img alt="Nilufer Ozmekik" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559807601p2/53701594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2938648360?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nilufer Ozmekik" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nilufer Ozmekik" href="/user/show/53701594-nilufer-ozmekik">Nilufer Ozmekik</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2938648360" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1312999557265169672">I wasn’t attending to the star giving auctions for too long but finally I FOUND A… ( oh no I couldn’t find an adjective to express my feelings about this book. Fantastic! No! Too weak! Extraordinary! No! Not emphasizing my emotions enough! Okay let’s get over this auction as I resume my brain storming to find the right words!)<br/><br/>One zillion stars… Did I hear three zillion! What the hell! Five gazillion! What! One jillion, one jillion! Okay two, three jillion! Oh the read head crazy lady already wro</span>
  <span id="freeText1312999557265169672" style="display:none">I wasn’t attending to the star giving auctions for too long but finally I FOUND A… ( oh no I couldn’t find an adjective to express my feelings about this book. Fantastic! No! Too weak! Extraordinary! No! Not emphasizing my emotions enough! Okay let’s get over this auction as I resume my brain storming to find the right words!)<br /><br />One zillion stars… Did I hear three zillion! What the hell! Five gazillion! What! One jillion, one jillion! Okay two, three jillion! Oh the read head crazy lady already wrote 5 squillion starred review check! SOLD!<br /><br />I still haven’t found an adjective to describe how I fell in love with this book and it will need to be removed from my hands with an operation at the hospital because I accidentally glued my fingers as an answer to my husband tried too hard to pull it back and force me to sleep. Sorry pal, too many books not enough time is motto of my life!<br /><br />The reasons for a passionate real reader to fall in love with this book are:<br /><br />-Amazing story telling, fast-pacing progression, heartbreakingly enjoyable, likable, adorable characterizations, satisfyingly well rounded improvisations!<br /> <br />-Main character Lou is a freaking WITCH falls in love with her own hunter, chausseur Reid! Yes, there is flaming, undeniable chemistry, forbidden, impossible, heart-wrecking, angsty, edgy love story! The enemies to lovers and becoming every adorable thing of each other kind of heart throbbing, sweet stories are always my big winners! <br /><br />Lou is witty, brave, tough, badass witch you want to choose to be on your side because she is more dangerous than she looks. And my dear Reid Diggory, charming, sweet chivalry in his shining fitting armor is one of the most loyal and genuine men in the earth. He still wants to protect Lou which is so noble intention as you consider the woman is already trained enough to protect herself as well.<br /><br />This is amazing journey took place in 18th century France! Do I need another reason to add for liking this book? O lala! Now I’m sipping my Sancerre that I saved for special occasions (I know my husband will kill me not wait for his birthday to change the bottle with cheap grape juice!) and absorbing each words slowly by touching the pages gently (I bought its ten hardcover copies to share it my friends but I decided I love this book so much and I’ll keep all copies with me! Please don’t tell my husband, I used his credit card that I borrowed to buy him plane tickets for his business trip which I didn’t! Shh!)<br /><br />This book makes you clap your hands with joy! It makes you smile, gives your soul a genuine laughter, brushes your heart gently and also makes you eat all your nails at the edgy parts and finally makes you jump up and down at your seat with its emotional turmoil.<br /><br />Oh I felt like non-stop talking PR person and exhausted already to find better words to describe my love about this book but I’m not good at talking. I’m a mediocre writer but I’m a quite lover of reading extra-amazing-fantastic books.<br /><br />THIS IS ONE of THEM AND SO FAR THIS YEAR’S BEST FANTASY BOOK I’VE EVER READ! HIGHLY RECOMMENDED NOT ONLY FOR GENRE FANS BUT ALSO FOR ALL GOOD READERS!<br /><br /><a href="https://niluferozmekik.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/nilylovestoread/" rel="nofollow noopener">instagram</a><br /><a href="https://www.facebook.com/nilufer.ozmekik" rel="nofollow noopener">facebook</a><br /><a href="https://twitter.com/NiluferOzmekik" rel="nofollow noopener">twitter</a></span>

<div id="review_2965495837" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2965495837" />
    <a title="jessica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica"><img alt="jessica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1509983330p2/10171516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2965495837?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="jessica" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica">jessica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2965495837" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13255576164081633383">for the first time ever, i picked up a book without knowing anything about it. i didnt read the synopsis, not the back cover, nothing. and i have no idea if thats why im rating this so highly - because everything was such an exciting surprise - or what, but wow. this had me hooked!<br/><br/>the first thing that i noticed right away was the writing. my gosh, this does not read like a debut novel. this feels as if its written by a seasoned fantasy author. its utterly divine. <br/><br/>and the content is sooo magical.</span>
  <span id="freeText13255576164081633383" style="display:none">for the first time ever, i picked up a book without knowing anything about it. i didnt read the synopsis, not the back cover, nothing. and i have no idea if thats why im rating this so highly - because everything was such an exciting surprise - or what, but wow. this had me hooked!<br /><br />the first thing that i noticed right away was the writing. my gosh, this does not read like a debut novel. this feels as if its written by a seasoned fantasy author. its utterly divine. <br /><br />and the content is sooo magical. its totally giving off massive salem witch trial vibes, but set in old france. there are some moments where the religion aspect of the anti-witch stance gets to be a bit much, but i understand why its included. it helps with some character arcs, so i get it. <br /><br />but overall, this surprised and excited me at every turn. i definitely need to start picking up books and going into them blind, because it proved to be such a wonderful reading experience! 10/10 would recommend! <br /><br /><b>↠ <i>4.5 stars</i></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13255576164081633383" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2972384027" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2972384027" />
    <a title="MischaS_" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12772859-mischas"><img alt="MischaS_" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585808485p2/12772859.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2972384027?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MischaS_" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MischaS_" href="/user/show/12772859-mischas">MischaS_</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=english">english</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=disappointment">disappointment</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=unsure-if-i-ll-continue-this-series">unsure-if-i-ll-continue-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=expected-something-else">expected-something-else</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=not-interested-in-the-romance">not-interested-in-the-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=amazing-cover">amazing-cover</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2972384027" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8492950343526444966">This was a rather hard review to write. I have to say that it seems that with hyped/popular books, it seems that I either love them or hate them; unfortunately, this was the latter. <br/><br/>This book having an average 4,15* and 4,11* friends' average rating, seemed like a sure good read. Especially since even people who I "always" agree with seemed to like this book, the thing is while many people recommended this book to me, I still cannot blame it on having too high expectations for it. I honestly did</span>
  <span id="freeText8492950343526444966" style="display:none">This was a rather hard review to write. I have to say that it seems that with hyped/popular books, it seems that I either love them or hate them; unfortunately, this was the latter. <br /><br />This book having an average 4,15* and 4,11* friends' average rating, seemed like a sure good read. Especially since even people who I "always" agree with seemed to like this book, the thing is while many people recommended this book to me, I still cannot blame it on having too high expectations for it. I honestly did not expect anything from this book. Yet, it did disappoint me. <br /><br />I have to put the only/most positive thing right here at the beginning; the cover is truly gorgeous. <br /><br />Back to why writing this review was hard, and it connects to why I found reading this book hard. It was hard to care for it. It took me a long time to finish; I fell asleep several times, I found different things to do rather than reading this. And when I was finished, it was hard to find the will to write this review because the book just left my mind. I usually think a lot about the books I read; I replay scenes in my mind etc. but not this one. I did not think about this book once since I finished it.<br /><br />I found the story building and the background setting lacking. There was so little. Clearly, it was inspired by France even if it's totally fictional land. And for some reason, characters drop French here and there. Why is it necessary to say that they had <i>chocolat chaud</i>? Just say hot chocolate. Why they suddenly "speak" French? It does not make the book or the setting more french. <br />Same with "they were hunters, Chasseurs." So, they were hunters, hunters [in French]. What? <br /><br />Also, since Belterra is clearly fictional why the religion is so clearly Catholic with the Bible and everything? It's just such a strange middle ground. On one hand, going full fiction creating a new kingdom but then sticking the Bible in there. <br /><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[So, basically, the reason why she got into this mess is that she needed to pee real bad. Yeah, she had a ring which makes her invisible, she knew that there would be a huge crowd and wanted to remain unseen. Seems like a splendid moment when to use the said ring. But now, she just goes there and hopes no one notices her. And I'm asking why!? It seems to make no sense. Why not use the ring now? Or any other time when she needed to be unseen. Why?<br />What's the point of the ring if clearly that's the right moment for it, but Lou does not use it just to "move" the plot. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />A few people told me that the romance part is the best thing about this book. I have to speak about it as well. (Btw, I just noticed that I did not mention anything about the characters so far.)<br />I don't like the romance part of this book; I don't get it. I don't see it. It feels very artificial. It does not help that I did not really feel them getting closer together more like deciding "we're married, so, we should care for each other and love each other." Did not really work for me.<br />Plus, Reid seemed to have a personality of a blank page which did not help much. <br />Note, I finished this review and only after that, I realised that I did not really talk about Lou. So, here I am with not much to say. She goes for a thief to a wife pretty fast, and while I like the glimpse, we got of her at the beginning of the book that person never returned. <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[As for the ending, Coco is just like "my aunt is La Voisin". and everybody is so shocked but why should the reader care about this revelation since this La Voisin was mentioned not once in the whole book? Sort of kills the supposed cliffhanger. (Yes, I know that La Voisin was a real person and that goes back to the sprinkling France into a clearly fictional land. Speaking French here and there and giving things and people French names does not make it France-like.)<br />Same at the beginning Lou was like "She's after me", and I'm so over the pronounce game. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />But since this review was so far rather negative, I would like to mention a few more things which were the reason why this has two stars from me and not one. <br />The magic system had potential. I was interested in the difference between the Dames Rouges and Dames Blanches since in the "legend" only the latter were mentioned. <br />And I could get behind Beau and Coco that seemed like a potential for a fun arc. But then the author was clearly pushing Ansel to the mix, and I cannot suffer through another book just to get a love triangle or Coco ending with Ansel. <br /><br />So, yes, this is me saying that I won't be continuing with this series. And yes, I know that this review is a mess, but I just cannot find the will to spend any more time trying to make it more presentable. <br /><br /><br />Reaction after finishing:<br /><br />Big Titty Liddy? What was even that? Who thought that that was a good idea?<br /><br />RTC but I can say that I was not a fan of this one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8492950343526444966" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2960327048" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2960327048" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2960327048?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062878045" href="/book/show/41453719-serpent-dove">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2960327048" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18173423506607508912"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584329758i/29113132._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>[2nd Read]<br/><br/>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>All the controversies and mixed reviews that have been surfacing the GR platform since the book was published made this re-read less fun. I kept thinking about the bad things people were saying. Enough to make me question myself, but not to the point where I didn’t . . . still enjoy the book.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b><br/>___________________________<br/><br/><b>[1st Read]<br/><br/>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>Ahh I love this book so freaking much!! and I’ve been walking on air since I finished it. This is an impressive debut </span>
  <span id="freeText18173423506607508912" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584329758i/29113132._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>[2nd Read]<br><br>4 Stars</b><br><br>All the controversies and mixed reviews that have been surfacing the GR platform since the book was published made this re-read less fun. I kept thinking about the bad things people were saying. Enough to make me question myself, but not to the point where I didn’t . . . still enjoy the book.<br><br><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b><br>___________________________<br><br><b>[1st Read]<br><br>4.5 Stars</b><br><br>Ahh I love this book so freaking much!! and I’ve been walking on air since I finished it. This is an impressive debut novel that doesn’t feel like one at all bcs of how outstanding the author’s writing craftsmanship is.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1532214986ra/26010384.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m not good with summarizing, but basically this book is about two sworn enemies who, after a stunt gone wrong, are forced into a matrimony. However, there’s more to this book than just the slow burn enemies to lovers blooming romance.<br><br>It has a distinct magic system, bloody action sequences, constant dilemmas between right and wrong, a strong female friendship, heart jolting plot twists, an unlikely alliance among different sets of characters, an alluring 17th century French inspired setting, and so much more.<br><br>Reading this book had been a living on cloud nine kind of experience. You know that stinging sensation you get in your chest when you feel excited and touched by something?? Well this book gave me lots and lots of that zap in my chest. I am now obsessed!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1570256144ra/28246612.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I would strongly recommend you to <b>READ THIS BOOK</b>!! But please don’t let the hype get to you. I would hate for it to ruin the surprise for you. Just start the book with an open mind, and let it do its job to wow you.<br>___________<br><br>【<b>CHARACTERS</b>】<br>___________<br><br><b><i>LOUISE le BLANC</i> is the REAL EFFING DEAL!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1580900687ra/28906845.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love her to the moon and back. She’s sassy, spunky, clever, strong, and independent. With the threat of her terrorizing past looming over her head and the <i>chasseur</i> incessantly hunting down for witches to burn, Lou’s safety hangs in the balance. I loved seeing her inner turmoil and how she slowly learned to view things from different perspectives, including that of her enemies. She’s so relentless in her pursuit to stay alive that she’s willing to do whatever it takes to survive. and I really admire this about her.<br><br><b><i>REID DIGGORY</i> is a SWOON WORTHY IDIOT!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1539774507ra/26461553.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That’s an insult laced with flattery if you ever heard one. His character lacks complexity, but I still liked him nonetheless. I mean, even <i>I</i> am not immune to pompous jerks with anger management issues. I found Reid’s hatred towards the witches to be a little unconvincing. A lot of his reasons came from what he saw being done to other people instead of his own personal traumatic experience. He was also raised to hate them, which I can admit is understandable but also really judgemental on his part.<br>_____________<br><br>【<b>RELATIONSHIPS</b>】<br>_____________<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1570260216ra/28246815.gif" width="500" height="310" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I LIVE FOR THIS SHIP!!</b> - The romance between Lou and Reid was everything!! I loved every single moment they spent together. Their banter was off the charts and super entertaining. Their tension and emotional complexity could use some improvement. Also, Reid’s inner turmoil when he found out Lou was a witch lasted too short. I think it’s because the author decided to reveal this detail to his character a little too late nearing the ending phase that Reid didn’t have enough time to be conflicted and reprocess his shattered belief. Regardless, their dynamic was satisfying.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1586613780ra/29274927.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>WHERE CAN I GET A BEST FRIEND LIKE COCO??</b> - She’s such a confident badass!! I loved seeing her friendship with Lou. She’s always so supportive and resourceful. Seeing these two teaming up and doing all kinds of shenanigans together really warmed my heart. We need more of this strong female friendship portrayal in books. They’re seriously BFFs goals!! Also, since the next book is going to explore more about Coco’s type of magic and her aunt’s coven, I hope to learn more about Coco and her past. I’m still undecided which one of Ansel and Beau I ship her with.<br>______________________<br><br>【<b>STORY AND OTHER ELEMENTS</b>】<br>______________________<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1580900687ra/28906846.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I would say that the first ⅓ of the book, the plot is relatively weak due to Lou and Reid’s new relationship and living arrangement. After hitting the halfway mark, the plot quickly arises during the climax of the story which marks the crack in Lou and Reid’s relationship as well as signals the coming war between the witches and the church. The ending phase is filled with action sequences. Ultimately, the book finishes with a somewhat solid ending that’s not entirely a cliffhanger but still holds a series of unanswered lingering questions. It’s enough to give us the anticipation for the sequel.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1580900687ra/28906847.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also have to give credits to the writing bcs the author’s brilliance really shone through. It’s easy to read and highly addictive. I feel like even if the other elements of the story were poorly done, I would’ve still kept reading bcs of the writing. The other thing I’d like to mention is the 17th century French inspired setting. I don’t know much about French, it’s history and culture. But what little of this book has shown really captivated me. I can only hope that the French ambiance will get more prominent and atmospheric in the next installment.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18173423506607508912" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2905544100" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2905544100" />
    <a title="Warda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30036082-warda"><img alt="Warda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593385153p2/30036082.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2905544100?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Warda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Warda" href="/user/show/30036082-warda">Warda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062878045" href="/book/show/41453719-serpent-dove">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30036082-warda?shelf=library-reads">library-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30036082-warda?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2905544100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16319145117828684094">A perfectly, adequate YA fantasy story about witches and witch hunters that left me feeling lukewarm. <br/>I went in with low expectations and came out of it not completely blown away by the story, which I expected. It was enjoyable, adorable, had its hilarious moments and the pacing was great. <br/>I got out of it what I wanted. <br/><br/>Even though the story lacked for me when it came to the world building and character development, I feel like the groundwork has been laid and I hope it’s build upon in the seque</span>
  <span id="freeText16319145117828684094" style="display:none">A perfectly, adequate YA fantasy story about witches and witch hunters that left me feeling lukewarm. <br>I went in with low expectations and came out of it not completely blown away by the story, which I expected. It was enjoyable, adorable, had its hilarious moments and the pacing was great. <br>I got out of it what I wanted. <br><br>Even though the story lacked for me when it came to the world building and character development, I feel like the groundwork has been laid and I hope it’s build upon in the sequel. There is so much more I would like to find out about the witches and some of the covens, of Morgane, more about Lou’s background and Reid’s journey to becoming a witch hunter.<br><br>I just need more. <br>YA fantasy stories have tendencies to be more plot focused. Character development scenes as well as world-building aspects are sprinkled into the story every now and again and that’s never enough for me to latch on. <br><br>I guess this all comes down to my taste preferences. I much rather read character driven stories than plot. <br><br>But I appreciated the romance, Lou’s feistiness, Reid’s devotion and loyalty to his faith and his grumpiness and story the author told about alluding to how women/witches were treated. <br><br>I might pick up the sequel. I really did enjoy the characters but I'll see what my mood will be like once the second book comes out. <br><br><br>———————————<br><br><br>Let’s be clear here: I’m in it for the romance. So that way if the fantastical aspect flops (since I’m not really all that into YA Fantasy anymore) I won’t be disappointed. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494351529ra/22707361.gif" width="310" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Buddy-reading with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/acourtofdreamers" rel="nofollow noopener">Asmaa!</a> We’re so ready to fangirl! 😍<br><br><i>Reading for the <b>#TomeTopple</b> readathon!</i></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3009919893" />
    <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson"><img alt="Whitney Atkinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550868411p2/14457130.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3009919893?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney Atkinson" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson">Whitney Atkinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=from-library">from-library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=superior-enemies-to-lovers">superior-enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=full-five-stars">full-five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=favs-of-2019">favs-of-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=smutty">smutty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3009919893" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18040368546752664799">the people who dislike this book are wrong, and that's just facts.<br/><br/>(i'm kidding--i love u and your reading tastes very much. muah.)<br/><br/>I'll preface this review by saying I typically don't enjoy books about witchcraft, so I was nervous going into this one. For me, books about magic walk a fine line of being too silly, which really takes me out of the world and makes it seem more childish instead of its intended intensity. But this book, its writing, and its world COMPLETELY captured me. <br/><br/>My favorite pa</span>
  <span id="freeText18040368546752664799" style="display:none">the people who dislike this book are wrong, and that's just facts.<br /><br />(i'm kidding--i love u and your reading tastes very much. muah.)<br /><br />I'll preface this review by saying I typically don't enjoy books about witchcraft, so I was nervous going into this one. For me, books about magic walk a fine line of being too silly, which really takes me out of the world and makes it seem more childish instead of its intended intensity. But this book, its writing, and its world COMPLETELY captured me. <br /><br />My favorite part of this book by far was the main character, Lou. If you loved Lila from A Darker Shade of Magic, you will absolutely love this book. Lou is crass and vulgar and charismatic and brave and doesn't care what other people think. Juxtaposed with a love interest and a world who are subdued and reserved, it made the narration so much fun. Lou was smart and talented and fun to learn about, which made her story that much more addicting. I also relate to using humor as a distraction technique, and the way Lou was written was so relatable. <br /><br />On top of that, the writing in this book was stunning. The world is French-inspired, and I love that I could see the corsets in my mind and the cobblestones and smog. This author is also great at detailing out the characters and their interactions, which makes me feel like I'm in the room with them when they're conversing. Though this book is written in first person dual POV, there's a distinct difference between the voices of the two characters, and I never had to double check to see who I was reading from. I for sure want to read everything Shelby writes in the future. <br /><br />Another interesting facet of this book (I could go on forever) is the whole conflict of witches vs the church. The conversations this book evokes about religion and corruption and fear are so nuanced and subtle, which I really applauded. Both from an external perspective and seeing how the characters develop and learn more about one another and shift their points of views to be more understanding and tolerant was so beautiful. I was actually crying for the whole middle section of this book because it was sad and touching and made me think a lot more than I had anticipated.<br /><br />Although this book is a definite far stars from me, I did find myself a little bit more impressed with the first half of this book than the last. Don't get me wrong, I devoured this 500 page book in nearly two sittings, but it felt like the first half was full of funny and cute and angsty moments, and then the last half of this book was a bit more subdued. The reveals weren't as shocking, the progression of the relationship wasn't as special, but I still like the direction it went. I wish the enemies to lovers plotline was fraught with a little bit more tension in the end, but that's more of a personal preference than an actual flaw of the book. <br /><br />But this book was glorious and I'm highly anticipating book two and that's that on that.</span>
