<div id="review_2902486627" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2902486627" />
    <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey"><img alt="Chelsea Humphrey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585613513p2/47207032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2902486627?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea Humphrey" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey">Chelsea Humphrey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780062977106" href="/book/show/52885133-serpent-dove">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47207032-chelsea-humphrey?shelf=library">library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47207032-chelsea-humphrey?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47207032-chelsea-humphrey?shelf=bookstagram-made-me-do-it">bookstagram-made-me-do-it</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2902486627" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11565997606504743836"><i>"A witch and a witch hunter bound in holy matrimony. There was only one way such a story could end-a stake and a match."</i><br/><br/>I don't know about you, but I find it is a rare day that the hype beast lives up to it's nature, and what a glorious feeling it is when a book lives up to the promises doled out by publishers and early reviewers alike. <i>Serpent & Dove</i> deserves every bit of praise that has been heaped upon it's name, and it will be a most excruciating wait for the second installment. If you have </span>
  <span id="freeText11565997606504743836" style="display:none"><i>"A witch and a witch hunter bound in holy matrimony. There was only one way such a story could end-a stake and a match."</i><br /><br />I don't know about you, but I find it is a rare day that the hype beast lives up to it's nature, and what a glorious feeling it is when a book lives up to the promises doled out by publishers and early reviewers alike. <i>Serpent &amp; Dove</i> deserves every bit of praise that has been heaped upon it's name, and it will be a most excruciating wait for the second installment. If you have become jaded by the seemingly carbon copied YA fantasies released over the past year, please do not harden your heart to this precious gem. Give me a moment of your time, and I'll try my hardest to convince you to take a chance on this scorching, twisty, romantic historical fantasy.<br /><br /><i>"Do not urge me to leave you or turn back from you." He trailed his fingers down my arm in slow, tortuous strokes. My head fell back on his shoulder, my eyes fluttering closed, as his lips continued to move against my neck. "Where you go, I will go. Where you stay, I will stay."</i><br /><br />Whatever I expected this story to be, it was not. How a book can be over 500 pages and not long enough, I'll never be able to explain, but something about the mixture of immersive atmosphere, jam packed action, and tender balance of emotion and secrets made this a winning combination. The narrative flips back and forth between Louise (a witch) and Reid (a witch hunter, or Chasseur), and the setting is a fantasy alternative to the 1700's era, though I will say the language felt very modern, which could be a hit or miss for some readers who are picky about these details. We are also introduced to a wonderful set of secondary characters, and if anyone tries to hurt my precious peach Ansel in this lifetime or the next, you'd better be prepared to hold my earrings. <br /><br /><i>Serpent &amp; Dove</i> is the kind of fantasy novel where we are dropped right in the middle of the action, and pieces of the magic system and setting are revealed as the story progresses, while also leaving other aspects to be expounded on in the sequel. Again, this may be a dealbreaker for some readers, but I found myself in tune with just enough knowledge to make the reading experience enjoyable, while also yearning to uncover more as the plot thickens. Also, I am pleased beyond words that the romance in this book is dreamy, steamy, and slow burning; in lieu of the popular instalove trope, this tale takes the route of swoon-worthy intimacy that is tested by time and trials. Did I mention it's super sexy with a strong message of consent? Totally here for it!<br /><br />Without diving into spoiler territory, you should know that there are twists, and then there are more twists, and then there are twists that we just have to think about until August of 2020 because <b>HOW DARE THE SEQUEL NOT BE AVAILABLE YET</b>?! Seriously, our group was mad texting upon finishing because we had SO many things to unpack from this read. Most of us are currently in a reading slump because this book was just that good. We talked about potential theories along the way, and we were all completely wrong with every guess. My emotions were off the charts, and my knee-jerk reaction was to start at the beginning and reread this book immediately upon finishing; it was that good.<br /><br /><b>Captivating. Refreshing.</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/40024139.Serpent___Dove__Serpent___Dove___1_" title="Serpent &amp; Dove (Serpent &amp; Dove, #1) by Shelby Mahurin" rel="nofollow noopener">Serpent &amp; Dove</a> has irrevocably restored my faith in the YA fantasy. If you're a lover of hate-to-love romance with a side of tense action and vivd imagination, please do yourself a favor and pick this one up. PS- the Barnes and Noble edition has an exclusive bonus scene featuring my baby Ansel, just saying.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11565997606504743836" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1689981606730511992"><i>WOWWW!!!</i> This was amazing! What a <b>stunning début</b>! I did <i>NOT</i> think, going into this, that it would be earning itself a place on my <i>favourites shelf</i>! If uni hadn't been such a hindrance (lol whyyy), I'd have absolutely torn through this in one sitting! If this is what Shelby Mahurin has to offer, I'm excited for what's to come in the future!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1568151892ra/28129714.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was an <b>enemies-to-lovers romance</b>, reminiscent of Matthias and Nina from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23437156.Six_of_Crows__Six_of_Crows___1_' title='Six of Crows (Six of Crows, #1) by Leigh Bardugo' rel='nofollow noopener'>Six of Crows</a> (aka my OTP of the series), but instead of <i>Grisha</i>, <b>Lou</b> was a <i>witch</i> an</span>
  <span id="freeText1689981606730511992" style="display:none"><i>WOWWW!!!</i> This was amazing! What a <b>stunning début</b>! I did <i>NOT</i> think, going into this, that it would be earning itself a place on my <i>favourites shelf</i>! If uni hadn't been such a hindrance (lol whyyy), I'd have absolutely torn through this in one sitting! If this is what Shelby Mahurin has to offer, I'm excited for what's to come in the future!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1568151892ra/28129714.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was an <b>enemies-to-lovers romance</b>, reminiscent of Matthias and Nina from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23437156.Six_of_Crows__Six_of_Crows___1_" title="Six of Crows (Six of Crows, #1) by Leigh Bardugo" rel="nofollow noopener">Six of Crows</a> (aka my OTP of the series), but instead of <i>Grisha</i>, <b>Lou</b> was a <i>witch</i> and <b>Reid</b> was a <i>witch hunter</i>. <br><br>Setting the book in a 17th century French<i>esque</i> world (as in the Loudun Witch Trials) really added to the <b>atmosphere</b> of the story. Also, the French student in me really enjoyed the smattering of French words throughout the book, hehe. <br><br>This <b>forbidden love story</b> was so compelling and addicting! However, I will say that this book is definitely <b>upper-YA</b>, as there is an explicit sex scene and tonnes of profanity, so be forewarned. <br><br>In this new world of <i>Belterra</i>, <b>witches are hunted</b> by order of the king. The <i>Chasseurs </i>are responsible for hunting them down and burning them at the stake. After fleeing her coven, <i>Les Dames Blanches</i>, Lou resorts to a life of <b>thievery</b> on the streets. Unfortunately, one bad event leads to another and she finds herself <b>forced into marriage</b> to the Chasseur, Reid. From then on, she struggles to <i>hide her identity</i> from her husband -- a man who would see her dead if he knew what she was -- while also coming to terms with her <i>growing feelings</i> for him. <br><br>This <b>pagan witchcraft</b> novel was so well done and perfect for this time of year, so I can't wait for the sequel to be released next year. I'd recommend it to fans of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22544764.Uprooted" title="Uprooted by Naomi Novik" rel="nofollow noopener">Uprooted</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/32824058.Strange_Grace" title="Strange Grace by Tessa Gratton" rel="nofollow noopener">Strange Grace</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42370636.The_Near_Witch" title="The Near Witch by Victoria Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">The Near Witch</a>.</span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2990114396?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja  - BibliophiliaDK ✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja  - BibliophiliaDK ✨" href="/user/show/3444336-maja---bibliophiliadk">Maja  - BibliophiliaDK ✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3444336-maja---bibliophiliadk?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3444336-maja---bibliophiliadk?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3444336-maja---bibliophiliadk?shelf=favourite-books">favourite-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2990114396" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11422568511430201002"><b>I DARE ANYONE TO NOT LOVE THIS BOOK! ❤️</b><br/><br/>Being stubborn as I am, I was hesitant about letting myself love this book because I saw how much others loved it (I am stupid like that!). So when I started I was hard at work trying to find flaws with it. And sure, I did find one or two, but soon they fled my mind completely - I was just swept up in this story! This is the first time since I was a teenager that I have stayed up waaaay past midnight because I couldn't stop reading! ❤️<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I promised to</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11422568511430201002" style="display:none"><b>I DARE ANYONE TO NOT LOVE THIS BOOK! ❤️</b><br /><br />Being stubborn as I am, I was hesitant about letting myself love this book because I saw how much others loved it (I am stupid like that!). So when I started I was hard at work trying to find flaws with it. And sure, I did find one or two, but soon they fled my mind completely - I was just swept up in this story! This is the first time since I was a teenager that I have stayed up waaaay past midnight because I couldn't stop reading! ❤️<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I promised to love and protect you"<br />"And I promised to love and obey you. We're both such pretty liars."<br />- Reid and Lou </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b> ❤️ THE THINGS I LOVED ❤️</b><br /><br /><u>Lou</u>: The first thing that started to break my resolve was Lou! She was the perfect heroine - cocky, brass and vulnerable. And I was really drawn to the fact that she was neither good nor bad, she was this 'gray' character, who was just trying to survive a war, that set 'black' against 'white'.<br /><br /><u>Reid</u>: Secondly, Reid started to get under my skin in the best of ways. At first I wasn't into his holy exterior, but as he softened up to Lou, so did I soften up to him!<br /><br /><u>Lou and Reid</u>: Yes, they do deserve a section on their own, because their relationship was just the cutest! It was so well-crafted and nicely developed, actually one of the best I have read in a long time. I especially loved the hate-turned-love aspect. Wonderful!<br /><br /><u>Transportation</u>: Books that have the power to transport me away from wherever I am while I am reading are the very, very best. This was one of those books! <br /><br /><u>Plot</u>: Though a bit thin at times (sorry), the plot was still, overall, very engaging and riveting! I especially loved how you are unsure of who the bad guys and who the good guys are!<br /><br /><u>Universe</u>: What fascinated me most about the world, this book was set in, was how closely it resembled 17th century France. That was actually a very interesting take on a YA fantasy novel. The magic was, sadly, a little confusing and lacking in explanation at times, but that is easily overlooked when combined with all the other goodness!<br /><br />Follow me for more book goodness: <a href="https://www.facebook.com/BibliophiliaDK/?modal=admin_todo_tour" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/BibliophiliaDK" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/bibliophiliadk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zainab" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zainab" href="/user/show/48759239-zainab">Zainab</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2935558489" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1486810559623844352">My dudes, this book was....<i>something</i>.<br/><br/><br/>Okay so the only time I actually like romance in a book is if it starts off with hate. Dude I love hate. So obviously I was very excited for this book and it did not disappoint- well at least the first 300 pages didn't.<br/>The thing is, I really liked Reid at first because I thought he was chivalrous and all but there's a difference between chivalry and being a dumbass and our beloved Reid is a cringey dumbass.<br/>The romance was sudden and cringey and made me want t</span>
  <span id="freeText1486810559623844352" style="display:none">My dudes, this book was....<i>something</i>.<br /><br /><br />Okay so the only time I actually like romance in a book is if it starts off with hate. Dude I love hate. So obviously I was very excited for this book and it did not disappoint- well at least the first 300 pages didn't.<br />The thing is, I really liked Reid at first because I thought he was chivalrous and all but there's a difference between chivalry and being a dumbass and our beloved Reid is a cringey dumbass.<br />The romance was sudden and cringey and made me want to puke. Maybe it's my INTP side, maybe the romance <i>is</i> awful. Reid is a very touchy guy like, dude, sheesh, back off.<br />The last 200 hundred pages are a bit of a mess. The 'twists' were just thrown in all together creating a big mush.<br /><br />Still, there are quite a few things I enjoyed about this book.<br />Lou and Coco's friendship is to die for. I actually enjoyed it more than the romance between Lou and Reid.<br />Then there is the whole witches thing. My dude that was <i>exciting</i>.<br />And last but not least, Lou. She is quirky and smart and a badass.<br />There's also some other bits but it'd get too spoilery.<br /><br />Writing this review taught me two things:<br />1- I did not hate this book as much as I thought I did.<br />2- I am one bitter hag.<br /><br /><a href="https://abookblog00787818964.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blog</a></span>

<div id="review_3006677126" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3006677126" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3006677126?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=0-in-my-library-read">0-in-my-library-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=marriage-of-convenience-ish">marriage-of-convenience-ish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=low-or-no-steam">low-or-no-steam</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=ya-fantasy">ya-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3006677126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14721229347216048356"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>I picked this up because I saw it being touted in some places around GR and booktube as a "racy" YA romance that was (perhaps) edgy enough for some people to feel it should have been classified more as New Adult a la ACOTAR. <br/><br/>And because I had a Barnes and Noble gift card burning a hole in my pocket. <br/>So I picked up this and <i>Ninth House</i>. <br/>And perhaps a couple other things. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571600001i/28325813.jpg' width='420' height='294' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It also felt very season appropriate to read about witches and buy black books with snakes on the covers. Very Hallowe</span>
  <span id="freeText14721229347216048356" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br>I picked this up because I saw it being touted in some places around GR and booktube as a "racy" YA romance that was (perhaps) edgy enough for some people to feel it should have been classified more as New Adult a la ACOTAR. <br><br>And because I had a Barnes and Noble gift card burning a hole in my pocket. <br>So I picked up this and <i>Ninth House</i>. <br>And perhaps a couple other things. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571600001i/28325813.jpg" width="420" height="294" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It also felt very season appropriate to read about witches and buy black books with snakes on the covers. Very Halloween/October of me, no?<br><br>But I digress. <br><br>As I was saying, I picked this up because I love me some racy. And because I also loved the premise of a witch marrying what amounts to a witch hunter.<br><br>And while I will say this book definitely had more swearing, "racy" language (for a YA), and a somewhat lukewarm sex scene, it didn't feel like anything I hadn't read before...but keep in mind, I'm also very forgetful these days. And not the target audience here. So take that as you will. <br><br>Regardless.<br><br>I thought the story itself was solidly entertaining, although nothing super extraordinary. The pacing was good and the world-building was decent. I will say that some of the characters felt slightly two-dimensional at times. <br><br>Most notably though, the relationship between Lou and Reid felt very groundless to me. They went from meeting and hating each other...to spending a week basically occupying the same room whilst doing their best to ignore each other...to being in love and boinking within a <i>very</i> short time period. It felt very sudden and shallow and I think Mahurin could have done a better job at laying the groundwork for their romance - and thus what amounts to the main focal point of this book. <br><br>Their "love" just didn't feel like it was palpable enough for me to believe that either one would feel the way they supposedly did during the events that occurred toward the end of the book. <br><br>Keeping in mind this is a debut series by a debut author, however, I have a good feeling about the potential for the next book in the series. This was definitely a strong debut and I look forward to more from this author.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14721229347216048356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2715240383" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4381311067719970404">Louise Le Blanc is a young witch with a fairly simple view of the world. Witches are good, Chasseurs are bad. <br/><br/>Good versus evil; there is no in between.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1568407522ra/28143780.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But when her own mother tries to kill her, Lou is forced to flee her coven. Trying to survive on her own, the world suddenly seems more complicated. <br/><br/>Maybe everything isn't as black and white as she thought?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576338828ra/28611258.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Reid Diggory has lived a very different life than Lou. As a Chasseur he abides by the creed '<i>Thou shalt not suffer a witch to live.'</i> <br/><br/>The Chasse</span>
  <span id="freeText4381311067719970404" style="display:none">Louise Le Blanc is a young witch with a fairly simple view of the world. Witches are good, Chasseurs are bad. <br><br>Good versus evil; there is no in between.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1568407522ra/28143780.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But when her own mother tries to kill her, Lou is forced to flee her coven. Trying to survive on her own, the world suddenly seems more complicated. <br><br>Maybe everything isn't as black and white as she thought?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576338828ra/28611258.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reid Diggory has lived a very different life than Lou. As a Chasseur he abides by the creed '<i>Thou shalt not suffer a witch to live.'</i> <br><br>The Chasseurs, employed by the Church, are essentially witch hunters. They are trained to fight for the downfall of all magic and the individuals who wield it.<br><br>When Reid and Lou are hastily forced into a marriage, he isn't aware that she is a witch, but it is certainly clear that she is not your average girl. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1576338828ra/28611259.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What could possibly go wrong?<br><br>In short, pretty much everything.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472571565ra/20209697.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Guys, I was so pumped to read this book based on early reviews, but in the beginning, I wasn't sold. <br><br>The pacing was super off for me and it took me until the halfway point to actually become engaged with the story.<br><br>This book is over 500-pages so that means I spent 250-pages trudging along just hoping it would get better.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441405451ra/16103802.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Luckily, for me, in the end, it did come around and I turned out enjoying the second half. <br><br>The final group of characters who joined together to battle the baddies was fun and I look forward to reading more of them together in the second book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450184248ra/17390766.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's right, I will be continuing on with this series!! <br><br>I wish I could give this a higher rating but personally, I felt the beginning portion could have done with some more editing.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485464507ra/21817987.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Again, however, the second half was stronger and I am intrigued enough to return to this world and see what happens with Lou and Reid!</span>

<div id="review_3331232899" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3331232899" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3331232899?book_show_action=true">May 11, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=2019-publications">2019-publications</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=witches">witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3331232899" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7848509384148046080">Serpent & Dove is one of those fantastic fantasy books that completely deserve being devoured, as slowly or as fast as you wish. It will increase your interest with each new chapter, so much that its 500 pages will have felt like 300 by the end. Shelby Mahurin doesn’t reinvent witches, but she does do something interesting with the concept and the use of magic. The forbidden love part sure was exciting, too, and I dare say I’m counting down the days until the release of book 2. <br/><br/>If I have one com</span>
  <span id="freeText7848509384148046080" style="display:none">Serpent &amp; Dove is one of those fantastic fantasy books that completely deserve being devoured, as slowly or as fast as you wish. It will increase your interest with each new chapter, so much that its 500 pages will have felt like 300 by the end. Shelby Mahurin doesn’t reinvent witches, but she does do something interesting with the concept and the use of magic. The forbidden love part sure was exciting, too, and I dare say I’m counting down the days until the release of book 2. <br /><br />If I have one complaint, it’s that the characters didn’t spend enough time outside of buildings and closed doors. But Shelby Mahurin doesn’t over-describe and she likes to make her characters talk with conviction, passion and even malice (hehe), so unless you somehow don’t end up being amused or intrigued by the idea of a witch and a witch-hunter marrying each other without knowing the truth about one another, I dare say add this title to your pile of books you want to get through during your time in isolation. (Maybe even at the top of the pile.)<br /><br /><a href="https://hitormissbooks.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/LolaReviewer" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a>Twitter</a> | <a>Instagram</a> | <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/105021852309973899120/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">Google+</a> | <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/hit-miss-books-12564715" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin’</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7848509384148046080" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2895224823" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2895224823" />
    <a title="Lucy Langford" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74034800-lucy-langford"><img alt="Lucy Langford" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518091381p2/74034800.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2895224823?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucy Langford" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucy Langford" href="/user/show/74034800-lucy-langford">Lucy Langford</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2895224823" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15539073382702009670"><i>”I was no one's sacrifice. Not then. Not now. Not ever.”</i><br/><br/>Still a fantastic read the second time around- I adore Lou as a character and I am eagerly anticipating the sequel towards the end of this year. <br/><br/>Original review:<br/><br/>I LOVED THIS!!! All the stars for this witchy goodness!!! 🧙‍♀️ <br/><br/><i>A witch and a witch hunter bound in holy matrimony. There was only one way such a story could end- a stake and a match.</i><br/><br/>The war between the witches and the church is ancient and ongoing. Louise is a witch who has runaway </span>
  <span id="freeText15539073382702009670" style="display:none"><i>”I was no one's sacrifice. Not then. Not now. Not ever.”</i><br /><br />Still a fantastic read the second time around- I adore Lou as a character and I am eagerly anticipating the sequel towards the end of this year. <br /><br />Original review:<br /><br />I LOVED THIS!!! All the stars for this witchy goodness!!! 🧙‍♀️ <br /><br /><i>A witch and a witch hunter bound in holy matrimony. There was only one way such a story could end- a stake and a match.</i><br /><br />The war between the witches and the church is ancient and ongoing. Louise is a witch who has runaway from her coven and takes cover in the city of Cesarine. She made the decision to forsake all magic and live off whatever she could steal. In the city of Cesarine it is dangerous to be a witch. They are hunted and they are feared. Those with magical powers, or even those who are friends with witches, are at risk of being tortured and burned at the stake. However, there are worse enemies for Lou other than the Church and it seems that these enemies are getting closer to finding Lou than she would like.<br /><br />Reid is a Chasseur- and a Captain at that. He is tasked as a witch hunter to hunt and find witches (obviously), gain information from them and to burn them to death at the stake. The one principle all Chasseur's follow is: THOU SHALT NOT SUFFER A WITCH TO LIVE. He has grown up in the Church and holds their views above anything else.<br /><br />When Lou’s and Reid's paths cross in unexpected ways, which could mean dishonour for Reid, it leads them into holy matrimony- an event which neither Lou nor Reid want to be part of. Living in close quarters with Reid and therefore being near other Chasseurs, Lou has to be careful with her magic lest she be detected and ultimately burned.<br /><br />This book had so many things that I enjoyed in it: a funny and fully realised heroine, evil witches, a jarring belief system in need of some changes, a deeply fascinating system of magic (especially used in a dark way), strong female friendships and many scenes of humour and wit. Lou was unapologetic in her ways, she was crass and loud and playful. From the start you know she is hiding from an enemy, but you just don't know who, and this kept me deeply intrigued in her story. On the other hand, Reid was "proper" and follows duty, never swearing and abiding by the churches rules. It was great to see these two characters interact with each other in their jarring ways. In addition, as Lou is a witch and Reid is a witch hunter, it was brilliant to see how their two mind sets were completely opposing and how these changed through out the book.<br /><br />Shelby Mahurin has done an excellent job at describing a world where the church is seen as the head of the state, with their views of witches and especially women are rigid and highly misogynistic. She also did a great job at describing the magic system as unique to this book (and sometimes among the witches!). One of the greatest things that I loved about this book was that most of the witches were malevolent and inflicted some of the strangest curses to the people of the city- the weirdness was fantastic.<br /><br />While this book does have romance in it, it is not the thing that kept me drawn to this book (I didn't mind the romance- its just not much of a genre that interests me). I mostly enjoyed how Reid and Lou would bicker and make fun of one another and I especially enjoyed the supportive friendship between Lou and Coco. <br /><br />While some of the magic was used for juvenile matters, I fully enjoyed the other aspects of this book. Overall, I need to read more books about witches as I fell in love with this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15539073382702009670" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0SHNvPDgTc7BggfhDTPb/yH6bNR8R1Re4EyEwz7n26MqCAsBJIDOc2VaxehB+4+aaZwRn1G4gvi3ZH4TGb61eg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7Imq1LjjXjcwCqu9XUf935ZX2fr2ZqjkXco/MyDbc/0XoGxpbIPdipTSabQRj6m63jGksduZfkIK4sXjB4IdJA==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer1575000617099251662">Shelby Mahurin grew up on a small farm in rural Indiana, where sticks became wands and cows became dragons. Her rampant imagination didn't fade with age, so she continues to play make-believe every day—with words now instead of cows. When not writing, Shelby watches the Office and obsesses over her Twitter feed. She still lives near that childhood farm with her very tall husband, semi-feral toddle</span>
  <span id="freeText1575000617099251662" style="display:none">Shelby Mahurin grew up on a small farm in rural Indiana, where sticks became wands and cows became dragons. Her rampant imagination didn't fade with age, so she continues to play make-believe every day—with words now instead of cows. When not writing, Shelby watches the Office and obsesses over her Twitter feed. She still lives near that childhood farm with her very tall husband, semi-feral toddlers, two dogs, and one cat. <br />​<br />Shelby's favorite books include A Court of Mist and Fury by Sarah J. Maas, Uprooted by Naomi Novik, The Night Circus by Erin Morgenstern, and, of course, Harry Potter.<br />​<br />Her debut novel, SERPENT &amp; DOVE, will release from Harper Teen in Fall 2019, with a sequel to come the following year. She is represented by Sarah Landis of Sterling Lord Literistic.</span>
